#### Microsoft Entra Privileged Identity Management (PIM)
> [LinkedIn Learning](https://www.linkedin.com/learning/microsoft-security-essentials-concepts-solutions-and-ai-powered-protection/microsoft-entra-privileged-identity-management-pim?u=76281980)

> [!transcript]- Transcript
>
> **[0:00](https://www.linkedin.com/learning/microsoft-security-essentials-concepts-solutions-and-ai-powered-protection/microsoft-entra-privileged-identity-management-pim?u=76281980&t=0)** - [Instructor] Microsoft Entra Privileged Identity Management or PIM helps organizations reduce the risk of excessive or misused access to critical resources.
>
> **[0:12](https://www.linkedin.com/learning/microsoft-security-essentials-concepts-solutions-and-ai-powered-protection/microsoft-entra-privileged-identity-management-pim?u=76281980&t=12)** Privileged roles like admin and owner have high-level access permissions to important resources in your organization.
>
> **[0:20](https://www.linkedin.com/learning/microsoft-security-essentials-concepts-solutions-and-ai-powered-protection/microsoft-entra-privileged-identity-management-pim?u=76281980&t=20)** If these accounts are compromised or misused, it can cause significant damage to your business.
>
> **[0:28](https://www.linkedin.com/learning/microsoft-security-essentials-concepts-solutions-and-ai-powered-protection/microsoft-entra-privileged-identity-management-pim?u=76281980&t=28)** So how do we manage the risk of too much or unnecessary access?
>
> **[0:34](https://www.linkedin.com/learning/microsoft-security-essentials-concepts-solutions-and-ai-powered-protection/microsoft-entra-privileged-identity-management-pim?u=76281980&t=34)** That's where Privileged Identity Management comes into play.
>
> **[0:39](https://www.linkedin.com/learning/microsoft-security-essentials-concepts-solutions-and-ai-powered-protection/microsoft-entra-privileged-identity-management-pim?u=76281980&t=39)** Microsoft Entra Privileged Identity Management can manage roles in Microsoft Entra like global administrator, user administrator, or billing administrator, roles in Azure, like owner, contributor, and user access administrator, and also make groups eligible for role assignments.
>
> **[1:03](https://www.linkedin.com/learning/microsoft-security-essentials-concepts-solutions-and-ai-powered-protection/microsoft-entra-privileged-identity-management-pim?u=76281980&t=63)** Microsoft Entra Privileged Identity Management or PIM offers some key capabilities, such as just in time or JIT access.
>
> **[1:14](https://www.linkedin.com/learning/microsoft-security-essentials-concepts-solutions-and-ai-powered-protection/microsoft-entra-privileged-identity-management-pim?u=76281980&t=74)** It means users get temporary access permissions only when they need to do some privileged operations like changing account information.
>
> **[1:24](https://www.linkedin.com/learning/microsoft-security-essentials-concepts-solutions-and-ai-powered-protection/microsoft-entra-privileged-identity-management-pim?u=76281980&t=84)** Approval and a justification can be required for activating privileged roles.
>
> **[1:31](https://www.linkedin.com/learning/microsoft-security-essentials-concepts-solutions-and-ai-powered-protection/microsoft-entra-privileged-identity-management-pim?u=76281980&t=91)** Time-bound, it means users can only use a privileged role within a defined time window.
>
> **[1:38](https://www.linkedin.com/learning/microsoft-security-essentials-concepts-solutions-and-ai-powered-protection/microsoft-entra-privileged-identity-management-pim?u=76281980&t=98)** Visibility, it refers to notifying relevant parties when the privileged role is activated.
>
> **[1:45](https://www.linkedin.com/learning/microsoft-security-essentials-concepts-solutions-and-ai-powered-protection/microsoft-entra-privileged-identity-management-pim?u=76281980&t=105)** An audit is available for track access history.
>
> **[1:50](https://www.linkedin.com/learning/microsoft-security-essentials-concepts-solutions-and-ai-powered-protection/microsoft-entra-privileged-identity-management-pim?u=76281980&t=110)** The general workflow of Privileged Identity Management starts with admins assign eligible roles to users for resource access.
>
> **[2:00](https://www.linkedin.com/learning/microsoft-security-essentials-concepts-solutions-and-ai-powered-protection/microsoft-entra-privileged-identity-management-pim?u=76281980&t=120)** Users activate eligible roles before performing privileged tasks.
>
> **[2:06](https://www.linkedin.com/learning/microsoft-security-essentials-concepts-solutions-and-ai-powered-protection/microsoft-entra-privileged-identity-management-pim?u=76281980&t=126)** Reviewers approve or deny role activation requests.
>
> **[2:10](https://www.linkedin.com/learning/microsoft-security-essentials-concepts-solutions-and-ai-powered-protection/microsoft-entra-privileged-identity-management-pim?u=76281980&t=130)** Before the role assignment expires, the user can request to extend it.
>
> **[2:16](https://www.linkedin.com/learning/microsoft-security-essentials-concepts-solutions-and-ai-powered-protection/microsoft-entra-privileged-identity-management-pim?u=76281980&t=136)** If it has already expired, the user can request to renew it.
>
> **[2:21](https://www.linkedin.com/learning/microsoft-security-essentials-concepts-solutions-and-ai-powered-protection/microsoft-entra-privileged-identity-management-pim?u=76281980&t=141)** And the history of privileged role assignments and activations is audited.
>
> **[2:29](https://www.linkedin.com/learning/microsoft-security-essentials-concepts-solutions-and-ai-powered-protection/microsoft-entra-privileged-identity-management-pim?u=76281980&t=149)** Now, let's look at Privileged Identity Management.

#### Microsoft Entra Global Secure Access
> [LinkedIn Learning](https://www.linkedin.com/learning/microsoft-security-essentials-concepts-solutions-and-ai-powered-protection/microsoft-entra-global-secure-access?u=76281980)

> **[0:00](https://www.linkedin.com/learning/microsoft-security-essentials-concepts-solutions-and-ai-powered-protection/microsoft-entra-global-secure-access?u=76281980&t=0)** - [Instructor] Microsoft Entra Global Secure Access helps organizations manage controlled access to software as service, SaaS applications, and private corporate resources.
>
> **[0:12](https://www.linkedin.com/learning/microsoft-security-essentials-concepts-solutions-and-ai-powered-protection/microsoft-entra-global-secure-access?u=76281980&t=12)** From a security point of view, it delivers the key capabilities of a security service edge solution.
>
> **[0:19](https://www.linkedin.com/learning/microsoft-security-essentials-concepts-solutions-and-ai-powered-protection/microsoft-entra-global-secure-access?u=76281980&t=19)** What is security service edge, or SSE?
>
> **[0:23](https://www.linkedin.com/learning/microsoft-security-essentials-concepts-solutions-and-ai-powered-protection/microsoft-entra-global-secure-access?u=76281980&t=23)** It's a cloud-based service that ensures safe access to the internet, cloud services, and private resources from anywhere.
>
> **[0:32](https://www.linkedin.com/learning/microsoft-security-essentials-concepts-solutions-and-ai-powered-protection/microsoft-entra-global-secure-access?u=76281980&t=32)** Security service edge includes several key services, Cloud Access Security Broker, CASB, or CASB, for securing cloud applications and data, Secure Web Gateway, SWG, for filtering internet traffic, blocking harmful websites, and enforcing corporate policies, and Zero Trust and Network Access, or ZTNA, for allowing remote users to access internal resources based on zero trust principles.
>
> **[1:08](https://www.linkedin.com/learning/microsoft-security-essentials-concepts-solutions-and-ai-powered-protection/microsoft-entra-global-secure-access?u=76281980&t=68)** While mapping these SSE services to Microsoft products, the matching solutions are Microsoft Defender for Cloud Apps, Microsoft Entra Internet Access, and a Microsoft Entra Private Access.
>
> **[1:26](https://www.linkedin.com/learning/microsoft-security-essentials-concepts-solutions-and-ai-powered-protection/microsoft-entra-global-secure-access?u=76281980&t=86)** Also, Microsoft Entra Global Secure Access is the unifying term that includes both Microsoft Entra internet access and private access.
>
> **[1:37](https://www.linkedin.com/learning/microsoft-security-essentials-concepts-solutions-and-ai-powered-protection/microsoft-entra-global-secure-access?u=76281980&t=97)** Here's a diagram from Microsoft, which provides an overview of Microsoft Entra Global Secure Access.

> **[1:44](https://www.linkedin.com/learning/microsoft-security-essentials-concepts-solutions-and-ai-powered-protection/microsoft-entra-global-secure-access?u=76281980&t=104)** We can see Global Secure Access unifies Microsoft Entra internet access and private access.
>
> **[1:51](https://www.linkedin.com/learning/microsoft-security-essentials-concepts-solutions-and-ai-powered-protection/microsoft-entra-global-secure-access?u=76281980&t=111)** It's built on zero trust principles.
>
> **[1:54](https://www.linkedin.com/learning/microsoft-security-essentials-concepts-solutions-and-ai-powered-protection/microsoft-entra-global-secure-access?u=76281980&t=114)** It works with identities, endpoints, and remote networks to route network traffic and provide secure access to various environments such as Microsoft 365 internet and private places.
>
> **[2:09](https://www.linkedin.com/learning/microsoft-security-essentials-concepts-solutions-and-ai-powered-protection/microsoft-entra-global-secure-access?u=76281980&t=129)** You can replace traditional VPNs with Microsoft Entra private access to securely connect to your corporate network from anywhere.
>
> **[2:19](https://www.linkedin.com/learning/microsoft-security-essentials-concepts-solutions-and-ai-powered-protection/microsoft-entra-global-secure-access?u=76281980&t=139)** To access private resources, you will create a special enterprise application.
>

>
> **[2:28](https://www.linkedin.com/learning/microsoft-security-essentials-concepts-solutions-and-ai-powered-protection/microsoft-entra-global-secure-access?u=76281980&t=148)** You can decide which resources to add to the container.
>
> **[2:33](https://www.linkedin.com/learning/microsoft-security-essentials-concepts-solutions-and-ai-powered-protection/microsoft-entra-global-secure-access?u=76281980&t=153)** The application has a network connector, acting as a bridge between private access service and the resources.
>
> **[2:41](https://www.linkedin.com/learning/microsoft-security-essentials-concepts-solutions-and-ai-powered-protection/microsoft-entra-global-secure-access?u=76281980&t=161)** There are two ways to set up a private access, quick access and per app access.
>
> **[2:49](https://www.linkedin.com/learning/microsoft-security-essentials-concepts-solutions-and-ai-powered-protection/microsoft-entra-global-secure-access?u=76281980&t=169)** For quick access, you create one Quick Access app and add resources to it.
>
> **[2:54](https://www.linkedin.com/learning/microsoft-security-essentials-concepts-solutions-and-ai-powered-protection/microsoft-entra-global-secure-access?u=76281980&t=174)** All resources share the same access policies applied to this app.
>
> **[3:00](https://www.linkedin.com/learning/microsoft-security-essentials-concepts-solutions-and-ai-powered-protection/microsoft-entra-global-secure-access?u=76281980&t=180)** You can use a fully qualified domain name, FQDN, IP addresses, IP ranges and ports to define your private resources.
>
> **[3:11](https://www.linkedin.com/learning/microsoft-security-essentials-concepts-solutions-and-ai-powered-protection/microsoft-entra-global-secure-access?u=76281980&t=191)** This information is called Quick Access App Segments.
>
> **[3:15](https://www.linkedin.com/learning/microsoft-security-essentials-concepts-solutions-and-ai-powered-protection/microsoft-entra-global-secure-access?u=76281980&t=195)** If you need more granular controls, for example, having different access policies for different private resources, you will use per app access.
>
> **[3:25](https://www.linkedin.com/learning/microsoft-security-essentials-concepts-solutions-and-ai-powered-protection/microsoft-entra-global-secure-access?u=76281980&t=205)** You can create multiple global secure access apps instead of a single Quick Access app.
>
> **[3:32](https://www.linkedin.com/learning/microsoft-security-essentials-concepts-solutions-and-ai-powered-protection/microsoft-entra-global-secure-access?u=76281980&t=212)** Then add your private resources to different apps based on their access requirements.
>
> **[3:38](https://www.linkedin.com/learning/microsoft-security-essentials-concepts-solutions-and-ai-powered-protection/microsoft-entra-global-secure-access?u=76281980&t=218)** Correspondingly, each app has its own app segments, which is why this method is called Per App Access.
>
> **[3:46](https://www.linkedin.com/learning/microsoft-security-essentials-concepts-solutions-and-ai-powered-protection/microsoft-entra-global-secure-access?u=76281980&t=226)** Microsoft Entra Global Secure Access also provides a dashboard with various widgets such as Global Secure Access Snapshot to summarize users, devices and the destinations with captured network traffic, alerts and notifications to monitor suspicious activities, usage profiling to display usage patterns for network traffic, cross-tenant access to show the number of users and the devices accessing other tenants, web category filters to highlight top categories of web content that are blocked or allowed, and a device status to show the active and inactive devices.
>
> **[4:33](https://www.linkedin.com/learning/microsoft-security-essentials-concepts-solutions-and-ai-powered-protection/microsoft-entra-global-secure-access?u=76281980&t=273)** Now let's look at Global Secure Access in the Microsoft Entra Admin Center.
>
> **[4:38](https://www.linkedin.com/learning/microsoft-security-essentials-concepts-solutions-and-ai-powered-protection/microsoft-entra-global-secure-access?u=76281980&t=278)** On the dashboard page, you'll find various widgets, for example, Global Secure Access Snapshot, alerts and notifications, usage profiling, and many others.
>
> **[4:53](https://www.linkedin.com/learning/microsoft-security-essentials-concepts-solutions-and-ai-powered-protection/microsoft-entra-global-secure-access?u=76281980&t=293)** To get started, you need to enable traffic forwarding profiles.
>
> **[4:58](https://www.linkedin.com/learning/microsoft-security-essentials-concepts-solutions-and-ai-powered-protection/microsoft-entra-global-secure-access?u=76281980&t=298)** Under Connect, click Traffic Forwarding.
>
> **[5:04](https://www.linkedin.com/learning/microsoft-security-essentials-concepts-solutions-and-ai-powered-protection/microsoft-entra-global-secure-access?u=76281980&t=304)** you can configure profiles for Microsoft Traffic, private access, and internet access.
>
> **[5:12](https://www.linkedin.com/learning/microsoft-security-essentials-concepts-solutions-and-ai-powered-protection/microsoft-entra-global-secure-access?u=76281980&t=312)** You can link conditional access policies to the profile and assign users and groups.
>
> **[5:21](https://www.linkedin.com/learning/microsoft-security-essentials-concepts-solutions-and-ai-powered-protection/microsoft-entra-global-secure-access?u=76281980&t=321)** Users can download the Global Secure Access Client to their devices.
>
> **[5:26](https://www.linkedin.com/learning/microsoft-security-essentials-concepts-solutions-and-ai-powered-protection/microsoft-entra-global-secure-access?u=76281980&t=326)** The client will tunnel traffic from the device to the Global Secure Access Service.

#### Threat protection with Microsoft Defender XDR

> **[0:05](https://www.linkedin.com/learning/microsoft-security-essentials-concepts-solutions-and-ai-powered-protection/threat-protection-with-microsoft-defender-xdr?u=76281980&t=5)** You may ask, "What is XDR?"
>
> **[0:09](https://www.linkedin.com/learning/microsoft-security-essentials-concepts-solutions-and-ai-powered-protection/threat-protection-with-microsoft-defender-xdr?u=76281980&t=9)** XDR stands for extended detection and response.

> **[0:13](https://www.linkedin.com/learning/microsoft-security-essentials-concepts-solutions-and-ai-powered-protection/threat-protection-with-microsoft-defender-xdr?u=76281980&t=13)** It's a type of security solution that collects data from various sources, like endpoint devices, emails, and cloud applications within your organization's environment, analyzes and detects threats and enables rapid response to those threats.
>
> **[0:33](https://www.linkedin.com/learning/microsoft-security-essentials-concepts-solutions-and-ai-powered-protection/threat-protection-with-microsoft-defender-xdr?u=76281980&t=33)** Microsoft Defender XDR is a suite of products that includes Microsoft Defender for Identity, which detects and investigates threats using active directory signals; Microsoft Defender for Endpoint, which offers protection, detection and incident response for endpoint devices; Microsoft Defender Vulnerability Management, which provides asset visibility, risk assessments, and a remediation for vulnerabilities and misconfigurations; Microsoft Defender for Office 365, which protects against threats from emails, links, and collaboration tools; and Microsoft Defender for Cloud Apps, which secures software-as-a-service, SaaS, applications
>
> **[1:25](https://www.linkedin.com/learning/microsoft-security-essentials-concepts-solutions-and-ai-powered-protection/threat-protection-with-microsoft-defender-xdr?u=76281980&t=85)** with visibility, data controls, and threat protection.

>
> **[0:06](https://www.linkedin.com/learning/microsoft-security-essentials-concepts-solutions-and-ai-powered-protection/microsoft-defender-for-endpoint?u=76281980&t=6)** It can be any device that communicates with a computer network, such as a laptop, desktop, server, virtual machine, phone, tablet, or internet of things, IoT device, like a security camera and a smart speaker.
>
> **[0:24](https://www.linkedin.com/learning/microsoft-security-essentials-concepts-solutions-and-ai-powered-protection/microsoft-defender-for-endpoint?u=76281980&t=24)** It's critical for organizations to secure their endpoints, because hackers can use a compromised device to penetrate the network and launch further attacks.
>
> **[0:36](https://www.linkedin.com/learning/microsoft-security-essentials-concepts-solutions-and-ai-powered-protection/microsoft-defender-for-endpoint?u=76281980&t=36)** Microsoft Defender for Endpoint is a comprehensive solution that helps organizations protect their endpoints.
>
> **[0:44](https://www.linkedin.com/learning/microsoft-security-essentials-concepts-solutions-and-ai-powered-protection/microsoft-defender-for-endpoint?u=76281980&t=44)** It offers various capabilities including Core Defender Vulnerability Management, which uses a risk-driven approach to manage endpoint vulnerabilities and misconfigurations; attack surface reduction, which verifies configuration settings and applies security controls like network protection and web protection; next-generation protection, which enhances antivirus functions by using techniques like behavior analysis, cloud-delivered protection, and a near-instant detection; endpoint detection and response, which helps security analysts better analyze and mitigate threats; automated investigation and remediation, or A-I-R, AIR,
>
> **[1:37](https://www.linkedin.com/learning/microsoft-security-essentials-concepts-solutions-and-ai-powered-protection/microsoft-defender-for-endpoint?u=76281980&t=97)** which automatically investigates alerts and performs remediation actions; Microsoft Secure Score for Devices, which helps you assess the current state, identify gaps, and take recommended actions; Microsoft Threat Experts, which offers a managed threat-hunting service; and management and APIs, which provides various APIs to share data and actions.
>
> **[2:08](https://www.linkedin.com/learning/microsoft-security-essentials-concepts-solutions-and-ai-powered-protection/microsoft-defender-for-endpoint?u=76281980&t=128)** You can access Microsoft Defender for Endpoint through the unified Microsoft Defender portal.

#### Microsoft Defender for Office 365
> [LinkedIn Learning](https://www.linkedin.com/learning/microsoft-security-essentials-concepts-solutions-and-ai-powered-protection/microsoft-defender-for-office-365?u=76281980)

> [!transcript]- Transcript

> **[0:00](https://www.linkedin.com/learning/microsoft-security-essentials-concepts-solutions-and-ai-powered-protection/microsoft-defender-for-office-365?u=76281980&t=0)** - [Instructor] Office 365 is a popular suite of productivity and collaboration tools, which includes applications like Word, Excel, PowerPoint, Outlook, and Teams.
>
> **[0:13](https://www.linkedin.com/learning/microsoft-security-essentials-concepts-solutions-and-ai-powered-protection/microsoft-defender-for-office-365?u=76281980&t=13)** Microsoft Defender for Office 365 integrates with Office 365 subscriptions and helps organizations protect against cyber threats.
>
> **[0:24](https://www.linkedin.com/learning/microsoft-security-essentials-concepts-solutions-and-ai-powered-protection/microsoft-defender-for-office-365?u=76281980&t=24)** There are some common attack techniques targeting Office 365, such as phishing.
>
> **[0:31](https://www.linkedin.com/learning/microsoft-security-essentials-concepts-solutions-and-ai-powered-protection/microsoft-defender-for-office-365?u=76281980&t=31)** Hackers send crafted emails to trick users into disclosing confidential information or taking unintended actions.
>
> **[0:41](https://www.linkedin.com/learning/microsoft-security-essentials-concepts-solutions-and-ai-powered-protection/microsoft-defender-for-office-365?u=76281980&t=41)** Malware distributed through email attachments or file downloads.
>
> **[0:47](https://www.linkedin.com/learning/microsoft-security-essentials-concepts-solutions-and-ai-powered-protection/microsoft-defender-for-office-365?u=76281980&t=47)** URL clicks.
>
> **[0:49](https://www.linkedin.com/learning/microsoft-security-essentials-concepts-solutions-and-ai-powered-protection/microsoft-defender-for-office-365?u=76281980&t=49)** Links in emails or messages lead to malicious websites, causing users to reveal credentials or install malware.
>
> **[0:58](https://www.linkedin.com/learning/microsoft-security-essentials-concepts-solutions-and-ai-powered-protection/microsoft-defender-for-office-365?u=76281980&t=58)** Microsoft Defender for Office 365 protects organizations from cyber attacks with three key capabilities.
>
> **[1:07](https://www.linkedin.com/learning/microsoft-security-essentials-concepts-solutions-and-ai-powered-protection/microsoft-defender-for-office-365?u=76281980&t=67)** Prevent and detect email and collaboration-based threats, using features such as anti-malware policies, filtering for spam in connections, safe attachments, alerts, attack simulation training, and integration with security information and event management, or SIEM solution.
>
> **[1:31](https://www.linkedin.com/learning/microsoft-security-essentials-concepts-solutions-and-ai-powered-protection/microsoft-defender-for-office-365?u=76281980&t=91)** Investigate threats with features such as threat exposure review, campaigns, threat tracker, and exchange message trace.
>
> **[1:44](https://www.linkedin.com/learning/microsoft-security-essentials-concepts-solutions-and-ai-powered-protection/microsoft-defender-for-office-365?u=76281980&t=104)** Respond to threats with features such as zero-hour auto purge, or ZAP, for malicious emails.
>
> **[1:52](https://www.linkedin.com/learning/microsoft-security-essentials-concepts-solutions-and-ai-powered-protection/microsoft-defender-for-office-365?u=76281980&t=112)** Automated investigation and response, or A-I-R, AIR, and automated responses in integrated security solutions, like SIEM.

### 6. 5. Cloud Infrastructure Security

#### Azure Virtual Network
> [LinkedIn Learning](https://www.linkedin.com/learning/microsoft-security-essentials-concepts-solutions-and-ai-powered-protection/azure-virtual-network?u=76281980)

> [!transcript]- Transcript
>
> **[0:00](https://www.linkedin.com/learning/microsoft-security-essentials-concepts-solutions-and-ai-powered-protection/azure-virtual-network?u=76281980&t=0)** - [Instructor] Network is the foundation of today's connected world.
>
> **[0:04](https://www.linkedin.com/learning/microsoft-security-essentials-concepts-solutions-and-ai-powered-protection/azure-virtual-network?u=76281980&t=4)** Before migrating your workloads from an on-premises environment to the cloud, it's critical to properly design your cloud network.
>
> **[0:15](https://www.linkedin.com/learning/microsoft-security-essentials-concepts-solutions-and-ai-powered-protection/azure-virtual-network?u=76281980&t=15)** Azure Virtual Network or VNet, enables organizations to build and manage their private network environment in the Microsoft Azure Cloud.
>
> **[0:25](https://www.linkedin.com/learning/microsoft-security-essentials-concepts-solutions-and-ai-powered-protection/azure-virtual-network?u=76281980&t=25)** It offers additional benefits such as scalability and availability.
>
> **[0:31](https://www.linkedin.com/learning/microsoft-security-essentials-concepts-solutions-and-ai-powered-protection/azure-virtual-network?u=76281980&t=31)** Network segmentation is a key concept in network security design.
>
> **[0:36](https://www.linkedin.com/learning/microsoft-security-essentials-concepts-solutions-and-ai-powered-protection/azure-virtual-network?u=76281980&t=36)** Basically, it means dividing a single large network into smaller parts.
>
> **[0:43](https://www.linkedin.com/learning/microsoft-security-essentials-concepts-solutions-and-ai-powered-protection/azure-virtual-network?u=76281980&t=43)** Why is this important?
>
> **[0:45](https://www.linkedin.com/learning/microsoft-security-essentials-concepts-solutions-and-ai-powered-protection/azure-virtual-network?u=76281980&t=45)** From a security standpoint, it helps minimize the impact of a breach.
>
> **[0:52](https://www.linkedin.com/learning/microsoft-security-essentials-concepts-solutions-and-ai-powered-protection/azure-virtual-network?u=76281980&t=52)** For example, if you have separate networks used by marketing, finance, and IT, attackers who penetrate one network may not be able to reach the others.
>
> **[1:04](https://www.linkedin.com/learning/microsoft-security-essentials-concepts-solutions-and-ai-powered-protection/azure-virtual-network?u=76281980&t=64)** We have talked about zero trust security model before.

>
> **[1:12](https://www.linkedin.com/learning/microsoft-security-essentials-concepts-solutions-and-ai-powered-protection/azure-virtual-network?u=76281980&t=72)** Network segmentation is an important component that supports zero trust.

>
> **[1:31](https://www.linkedin.com/learning/microsoft-security-essentials-concepts-solutions-and-ai-powered-protection/azure-virtual-network?u=76281980&t=91)** For example, a typical three tier web application has a presentation tier, application tier, and the database tier.
>

>
> **[1:51](https://www.linkedin.com/learning/microsoft-security-essentials-concepts-solutions-and-ai-powered-protection/azure-virtual-network?u=76281980&t=111)** Azure Virtual Network helps you implement a network segmentation easily.

#### Azure network security group
> [LinkedIn Learning](https://www.linkedin.com/learning/microsoft-security-essentials-concepts-solutions-and-ai-powered-protection/azure-network-security-group?u=76281980)

> [!transcript]- Transcript
>
> **[0:00](https://www.linkedin.com/learning/microsoft-security-essentials-concepts-solutions-and-ai-powered-protection/azure-network-security-group?u=76281980&t=0)** - [Narrator] A Network Security Group is an Azure service that filters network layer traffic within your virtual networks.
>
> **[0:08](https://www.linkedin.com/learning/microsoft-security-essentials-concepts-solutions-and-ai-powered-protection/azure-network-security-group?u=76281980&t=8)** After creating a network security group, or NSG, you can associate it with multiple subnets or network interfaces.
>
> **[0:17](https://www.linkedin.com/learning/microsoft-security-essentials-concepts-solutions-and-ai-powered-protection/azure-network-security-group?u=76281980&t=17)** So the same network security rules are applied to each of them.
>
> **[0:23](https://www.linkedin.com/learning/microsoft-security-essentials-concepts-solutions-and-ai-powered-protection/azure-network-security-group?u=76281980&t=23)** To create an NSG, you need to define security rules for both inbound and outbound network traffic.
>
> **[0:30](https://www.linkedin.com/learning/microsoft-security-essentials-concepts-solutions-and-ai-powered-protection/azure-network-security-group?u=76281980&t=30)** Here's an example of some default security rules used in NSGs.
>
> **[0:37](https://www.linkedin.com/learning/microsoft-security-essentials-concepts-solutions-and-ai-powered-protection/azure-network-security-group?u=76281980&t=37)** Each rule contains several properties, including priority presented by a number.
>
> **[0:44](https://www.linkedin.com/learning/microsoft-security-essentials-concepts-solutions-and-ai-powered-protection/azure-network-security-group?u=76281980&t=44)** The lower the number, the higher the priority.
>
> **[0:47](https://www.linkedin.com/learning/microsoft-security-essentials-concepts-solutions-and-ai-powered-protection/azure-network-security-group?u=76281980&t=47)** Meaning this rule will be assessed earlier.
>
> **[0:51](https://www.linkedin.com/learning/microsoft-security-essentials-concepts-solutions-and-ai-powered-protection/azure-network-security-group?u=76281980&t=51)** Once a rule matches the traffic, the process stops, and the remaining low priority-rules are skipped.
>
> **[0:59](https://www.linkedin.com/learning/microsoft-security-essentials-concepts-solutions-and-ai-powered-protection/azure-network-security-group?u=76281980&t=59)** Rule name, it should be unique and reflect its purpose.
>
> **[1:03](https://www.linkedin.com/learning/microsoft-security-essentials-concepts-solutions-and-ai-powered-protection/azure-network-security-group?u=76281980&t=63)** Port, it can be a single port number, like 80, or a range of ports.
>
> **[1:10](https://www.linkedin.com/learning/microsoft-security-essentials-concepts-solutions-and-ai-powered-protection/azure-network-security-group?u=76281980&t=70)** Network protocol, such as TCP, UDP, or any.
>
> **[1:16](https://www.linkedin.com/learning/microsoft-security-essentials-concepts-solutions-and-ai-powered-protection/azure-network-security-group?u=76281980&t=76)** Network traffic source and a destination.
>
> **[1:20](https://www.linkedin.com/learning/microsoft-security-essentials-concepts-solutions-and-ai-powered-protection/azure-network-security-group?u=76281980&t=80)** This can be an IP address, a range of IP addresses, a service tag, or application security groups.
>
> **[1:29](https://www.linkedin.com/learning/microsoft-security-essentials-concepts-solutions-and-ai-powered-protection/azure-network-security-group?u=76281980&t=89)** And finally, action.
>
> **[1:31](https://www.linkedin.com/learning/microsoft-security-essentials-concepts-solutions-and-ai-powered-protection/azure-network-security-group?u=76281980&t=91)** Do you want to allow or deny the traffic if the rule is applied?
>
> **[1:37](https://www.linkedin.com/learning/microsoft-security-essentials-concepts-solutions-and-ai-powered-protection/azure-network-security-group?u=76281980&t=97)** we can see the rule, allow Vnet inbound allows all inbound traffic with any ports and any protocols within the virtual network.
>
> **[1:47](https://www.linkedin.com/learning/microsoft-security-essentials-concepts-solutions-and-ai-powered-protection/azure-network-security-group?u=76281980&t=107)** However, there's another rule, deny all inbound, that denies all inbound traffic.
>
> **[1:54](https://www.linkedin.com/learning/microsoft-security-essentials-concepts-solutions-and-ai-powered-protection/azure-network-security-group?u=76281980&t=114)** So which rule will be applied?
>
> **[1:57](https://www.linkedin.com/learning/microsoft-security-essentials-concepts-solutions-and-ai-powered-protection/azure-network-security-group?u=76281980&t=117)** We need to check their priority numbers.
>
> **[2:00](https://www.linkedin.com/learning/microsoft-security-essentials-concepts-solutions-and-ai-powered-protection/azure-network-security-group?u=76281980&t=120)** Since they allow Vnet inbound rule has a lower number, it will be applied.
>
> **[2:07](https://www.linkedin.com/learning/microsoft-security-essentials-concepts-solutions-and-ai-powered-protection/azure-network-security-group?u=76281980&t=127)** The same logic also applies to outbound security rules.

#### Azure Firewall
> [LinkedIn Learning](https://www.linkedin.com/learning/microsoft-security-essentials-concepts-solutions-and-ai-powered-protection/azure-firewall?u=76281980)

> [!transcript]- Transcript
>
> **[0:00](https://www.linkedin.com/learning/microsoft-security-essentials-concepts-solutions-and-ai-powered-protection/azure-firewall?u=76281980&t=0)** - [Instructor] Azure Firewall is a managed cloud-based network security service provided by Microsoft Azure.
>
> **[0:08](https://www.linkedin.com/learning/microsoft-security-essentials-concepts-solutions-and-ai-powered-protection/azure-firewall?u=76281980&t=8)** Firewalls are classic security controls.
>
> **[0:11](https://www.linkedin.com/learning/microsoft-security-essentials-concepts-solutions-and-ai-powered-protection/azure-firewall?u=76281980&t=11)** They're widely used to separate external networks from internal networks in on-premises environments.
>
> **[0:19](https://www.linkedin.com/learning/microsoft-security-essentials-concepts-solutions-and-ai-powered-protection/azure-firewall?u=76281980&t=19)** Firewalls monitor and filter inbound and outbound network traffic based on predefined security policies or rules.
>
> **[0:28](https://www.linkedin.com/learning/microsoft-security-essentials-concepts-solutions-and-ai-powered-protection/azure-firewall?u=76281980&t=28)** However, as organizations migrate their workloads to the cloud, traditional firewalls face challenges in meeting the demands of hybrid environments, spanning both on-premises and a cloud infrastructure.
>
> **[0:44](https://www.linkedin.com/learning/microsoft-security-essentials-concepts-solutions-and-ai-powered-protection/azure-firewall?u=76281980&t=44)** This is where Azure Firewall comes into play.
>
> **[0:47](https://www.linkedin.com/learning/microsoft-security-essentials-concepts-solutions-and-ai-powered-protection/azure-firewall?u=76281980&t=47)** You have workloads running Azure Virtual Networks.
>
> **[0:51](https://www.linkedin.com/learning/microsoft-security-essentials-concepts-solutions-and-ai-powered-protection/azure-firewall?u=76281980&t=51)** They need to communicate with the resources on the internet and within your on-premises environment.
>
> **[0:58](https://www.linkedin.com/learning/microsoft-security-essentials-concepts-solutions-and-ai-powered-protection/azure-firewall?u=76281980&t=58)** Azure Firewall access a centralized network security control to filter the traffic among all entities.
>
> **[1:07](https://www.linkedin.com/learning/microsoft-security-essentials-concepts-solutions-and-ai-powered-protection/azure-firewall?u=76281980&t=67)** It also provides additional capabilities, such as monitoring both network and application network traffic, including protocols like HTTPS, building high availability to ensure continuous operations, tracking states of active connections to make decisions based on traffic context, supporting source and destination Network Address Translation, or NAT, to manage and secure traffic between the internet and your private resources, and integration with many other Azure services, like Azure Virtual Networks, Azure Policy, and Azure Monitor.
>
> **[1:53](https://www.linkedin.com/learning/microsoft-security-essentials-concepts-solutions-and-ai-powered-protection/azure-firewall?u=76281980&t=113)** Moreover, Azure Firewall is integrated with [[Microsoft Security Copilot]], an AI-powered assistant for security analysts.
>
> **[2:03](https://www.linkedin.com/learning/microsoft-security-essentials-concepts-solutions-and-ai-powered-protection/azure-firewall?u=76281980&t=123)** By enabling the Azure Firewall plugin, you can use prompts to access its capabilities in [[Microsoft Security Copilot]], such as searching across firewalls for intrusion detection and prevention signatures, or asking Copilot to generate recommendations to secure your environment using Azure Firewall.
>
> **[2:27](https://www.linkedin.com/learning/microsoft-security-essentials-concepts-solutions-and-ai-powered-protection/azure-firewall?u=76281980&t=147)** When speaking of network security services in Azure, you may wonder, "What's the difference between an Azure Firewall and an Azure Network Security Group or NSG?"
>
> **[2:39](https://www.linkedin.com/learning/microsoft-security-essentials-concepts-solutions-and-ai-powered-protection/azure-firewall?u=76281980&t=159)** It seems both of them can filter network traffic.
>
> **[2:44](https://www.linkedin.com/learning/microsoft-security-essentials-concepts-solutions-and-ai-powered-protection/azure-firewall?u=76281980&t=164)** The key differences are Azure Firewall is a centralized service to provide a protection across variance subscriptions and virtual networks.
>
> **[2:55](https://www.linkedin.com/learning/microsoft-security-essentials-concepts-solutions-and-ai-powered-protection/azure-firewall?u=76281980&t=175)** Network Security Groups work within virtual networks in each subscription.
>
> **[3:01](https://www.linkedin.com/learning/microsoft-security-essentials-concepts-solutions-and-ai-powered-protection/azure-firewall?u=76281980&t=181)** Azure Firewall can work with both network and application-level traffic.
>
> **[3:07](https://www.linkedin.com/learning/microsoft-security-essentials-concepts-solutions-and-ai-powered-protection/azure-firewall?u=76281980&t=187)** Network Security Groups filter network-layer traffic.
>
> **[3:12](https://www.linkedin.com/learning/microsoft-security-essentials-concepts-solutions-and-ai-powered-protection/azure-firewall?u=76281980&t=192)** You can combine Azure Firewalls and Network Security Groups in your cloud security architecture to implement a defense-in-depth strategy.

#### Azure Web Application Firewall
> [LinkedIn Learning](https://www.linkedin.com/learning/microsoft-security-essentials-concepts-solutions-and-ai-powered-protection/azure-web-application-firewall?u=76281980)

> [!transcript]- Transcript
>
> **[0:00](https://www.linkedin.com/learning/microsoft-security-essentials-concepts-solutions-and-ai-powered-protection/azure-web-application-firewall?u=76281980&t=0)** - [Narrator] Let's look at Azure Web Application Firewall.
>
> **[0:04](https://www.linkedin.com/learning/microsoft-security-essentials-concepts-solutions-and-ai-powered-protection/azure-web-application-firewall?u=76281980&t=4)** Web applications are widely used today, however, they have all kinds of vulnerabilities that attackers can exploit.
>
> **[0:13](https://www.linkedin.com/learning/microsoft-security-essentials-concepts-solutions-and-ai-powered-protection/azure-web-application-firewall?u=76281980&t=13)** For example, the Open Web Application Security Project, OWASP, is an international non-profit organization that works to improve application security.
>
> **[0:24](https://www.linkedin.com/learning/microsoft-security-essentials-concepts-solutions-and-ai-powered-protection/azure-web-application-firewall?u=76281980&t=24)** OWASP list top 10 security risks for web applications, such as broken access control injection and insecure design.
>
> **[0:35](https://www.linkedin.com/learning/microsoft-security-essentials-concepts-solutions-and-ai-powered-protection/azure-web-application-firewall?u=76281980&t=35)** Developers may spend significant time and effort trying to identify and mitigate application vulnerabilities.
>
> **[0:43](https://www.linkedin.com/learning/microsoft-security-essentials-concepts-solutions-and-ai-powered-protection/azure-web-application-firewall?u=76281980&t=43)** How can we add another layer of protection for web applications and enable developers to focus more on functionality?
>
> **[0:52](https://www.linkedin.com/learning/microsoft-security-essentials-concepts-solutions-and-ai-powered-protection/azure-web-application-firewall?u=76281980&t=52)** One possible solution is to use a web application firewall, or WAF.
>
> **[0:58](https://www.linkedin.com/learning/microsoft-security-essentials-concepts-solutions-and-ai-powered-protection/azure-web-application-firewall?u=76281980&t=58)** A WAF is placed between visitors and web apps.
>
> **[1:02](https://www.linkedin.com/learning/microsoft-security-essentials-concepts-solutions-and-ai-powered-protection/azure-web-application-firewall?u=76281980&t=62)** It works like a firewall to monitor and filter application requests.
>
> **[1:08](https://www.linkedin.com/learning/microsoft-security-essentials-concepts-solutions-and-ai-powered-protection/azure-web-application-firewall?u=76281980&t=68)** A WAF blocks web attacks targeting common application vulnerabilities.
>
> **[1:14](https://www.linkedin.com/learning/microsoft-security-essentials-concepts-solutions-and-ai-powered-protection/azure-web-application-firewall?u=76281980&t=74)** It only allows a valid request to interact with web apps.
>
> **[1:20](https://www.linkedin.com/learning/microsoft-security-essentials-concepts-solutions-and-ai-powered-protection/azure-web-application-firewall?u=76281980&t=80)** Azure Web Application Firewall provides centralized protection for web apps, so organizations can manage and patch vulnerabilities in one place, instead of working on each web application You can deploy Azure WAF with Azure Application Gateway, Azure Front Door, and Azure Content Delivery Network, or CDN.
>
> **[1:46](https://www.linkedin.com/learning/microsoft-security-essentials-concepts-solutions-and-ai-powered-protection/azure-web-application-firewall?u=76281980&t=106)** Azure WAF also helps defend against distributed denial of service, DDoS, attacks targeting applications.
>
> **[1:55](https://www.linkedin.com/learning/microsoft-security-essentials-concepts-solutions-and-ai-powered-protection/azure-web-application-firewall?u=76281980&t=115)** Moreover, Azure Web Application Firewall is integrated with [[Microsoft Security Copilot]], an AI-powered assistant for security analysts.
>
> **[2:06](https://www.linkedin.com/learning/microsoft-security-essentials-concepts-solutions-and-ai-powered-protection/azure-web-application-firewall?u=76281980&t=126)** You can use prompts to access its capabilities in [[Microsoft Security Copilot]], such as getting details of SQL injection or cross-site script attacks blocked by Azure Web Application Firewall.

#### Azure DDoS Protection
> [LinkedIn Learning](https://www.linkedin.com/learning/microsoft-security-essentials-concepts-solutions-and-ai-powered-protection/azure-ddos-protection?u=76281980)

> [!transcript]- Transcript
>
> **[0:00](https://www.linkedin.com/learning/microsoft-security-essentials-concepts-solutions-and-ai-powered-protection/azure-ddos-protection?u=76281980&t=0)** - [Instructor] Let's talk about Azure DDoS Protection.
>
> **[0:04](https://www.linkedin.com/learning/microsoft-security-essentials-concepts-solutions-and-ai-powered-protection/azure-ddos-protection?u=76281980&t=4)** First of all, what is DDoS?
>
> **[0:08](https://www.linkedin.com/learning/microsoft-security-essentials-concepts-solutions-and-ai-powered-protection/azure-ddos-protection?u=76281980&t=8)** DDoS stands for distributed denial of service.
>
> **[0:12](https://www.linkedin.com/learning/microsoft-security-essentials-concepts-solutions-and-ai-powered-protection/azure-ddos-protection?u=76281980&t=12)** It's a common type of cyber attack that aims to take down your services.
>
> **[0:18](https://www.linkedin.com/learning/microsoft-security-essentials-concepts-solutions-and-ai-powered-protection/azure-ddos-protection?u=76281980&t=18)** The word distributed indicates that attacks come from multiple sources.
>
> **[0:24](https://www.linkedin.com/learning/microsoft-security-essentials-concepts-solutions-and-ai-powered-protection/azure-ddos-protection?u=76281980&t=24)** For example, in a well-known DDoS attack, hackers used millions of compromised IoT devices to simultaneously send a request to an online service, eventually causing it to shut down.
>
> **[0:39](https://www.linkedin.com/learning/microsoft-security-essentials-concepts-solutions-and-ai-powered-protection/azure-ddos-protection?u=76281980&t=39)** There are some common types of DDoS attacks, including volume-based attacks that send numerous requests to overwhelm network bandwidth, blocking the traffic for legitimate requests.
>
> **[0:54](https://www.linkedin.com/learning/microsoft-security-essentials-concepts-solutions-and-ai-powered-protection/azure-ddos-protection?u=76281980&t=54)** Protocol-based attacks that flood specific protocols at the network and the transport layers to disrupt the service.
>
> **[1:03](https://www.linkedin.com/learning/microsoft-security-essentials-concepts-solutions-and-ai-powered-protection/azure-ddos-protection?u=76281980&t=63)** For example, ping flood or ICMP flood.
>
> **[1:08](https://www.linkedin.com/learning/microsoft-security-essentials-concepts-solutions-and-ai-powered-protection/azure-ddos-protection?u=76281980&t=68)** And the resource or application attacks that target the application layer to exhaust the available resources.
>
> **[1:16](https://www.linkedin.com/learning/microsoft-security-essentials-concepts-solutions-and-ai-powered-protection/azure-ddos-protection?u=76281980&t=76)** For example, HTTP flood or SQL injection.
>
> **[1:21](https://www.linkedin.com/learning/microsoft-security-essentials-concepts-solutions-and-ai-powered-protection/azure-ddos-protection?u=76281980&t=81)** Azure DDoS Protection specifically addresses the first two types of DDoS attacks at the network and the transport layers.
>
> **[1:32](https://www.linkedin.com/learning/microsoft-security-essentials-concepts-solutions-and-ai-powered-protection/azure-ddos-protection?u=76281980&t=92)** This is a diagram from Microsoft that illustrates the role of Azure DDoS Protection.
>
> **[1:39](https://www.linkedin.com/learning/microsoft-security-essentials-concepts-solutions-and-ai-powered-protection/azure-ddos-protection?u=76281980&t=99)** It helps organizations protect their services by continuously monitoring network traffic, intelligently tuning the traffic profiling, blocking detected DDoS attacks, and generating alerts.
>
> **[1:56](https://www.linkedin.com/learning/microsoft-security-essentials-concepts-solutions-and-ai-powered-protection/azure-ddos-protection?u=76281980&t=116)** As Azure DDoS Protection provides at network and transport layers, to fully cover all types of DDoS attacks, it's recommended to add Azure Web Application Firewall or WAF to defend against application layer DDoS attacks.

#### Azure Bastion
> [LinkedIn Learning](https://www.linkedin.com/learning/microsoft-security-essentials-concepts-solutions-and-ai-powered-protection/azure-bastion?u=76281980)

> [!transcript]- Transcript
>
> **[0:00](https://www.linkedin.com/learning/microsoft-security-essentials-concepts-solutions-and-ai-powered-protection/azure-bastion?u=76281980&t=0)** - [Instructor] Azure Bastion provides secure access to virtual machines directly from the Azure portal.
>
> **[0:07](https://www.linkedin.com/learning/microsoft-security-essentials-concepts-solutions-and-ai-powered-protection/azure-bastion?u=76281980&t=7)** For example, suppose your organization has virtual machines running in a virtual network within the Azure Cloud.
>
> **[0:15](https://www.linkedin.com/learning/microsoft-security-essentials-concepts-solutions-and-ai-powered-protection/azure-bastion?u=76281980&t=15)** Your administrator needs remote access to these virtual machines for maintenance tasks.
>
> **[0:22](https://www.linkedin.com/learning/microsoft-security-essentials-concepts-solutions-and-ai-powered-protection/azure-bastion?u=76281980&t=22)** One common way is to assign a public IP address to each virtual machine.
>
> **[0:26](https://www.linkedin.com/learning/microsoft-security-essentials-concepts-solutions-and-ai-powered-protection/azure-bastion?u=76281980&t=26)** Then, the admin uses RDP or SSH protocols to connect to these public IPs.
>
> **[0:34](https://www.linkedin.com/learning/microsoft-security-essentials-concepts-solutions-and-ai-powered-protection/azure-bastion?u=76281980&t=34)** However, it brings two immediate concerns.
>
> **[0:37](https://www.linkedin.com/learning/microsoft-security-essentials-concepts-solutions-and-ai-powered-protection/azure-bastion?u=76281980&t=37)** You need to allocate many public IPs and you need to loosen your network security rules to allow RDP or SSH access from the internet.
>
> **[0:50](https://www.linkedin.com/learning/microsoft-security-essentials-concepts-solutions-and-ai-powered-protection/azure-bastion?u=76281980&t=50)** This approach would expand the attack surface and increase your workload.
>
> **[0:56](https://www.linkedin.com/learning/microsoft-security-essentials-concepts-solutions-and-ai-powered-protection/azure-bastion?u=76281980&t=56)** This is where Azure Bastion can help.
>
> **[0:59](https://www.linkedin.com/learning/microsoft-security-essentials-concepts-solutions-and-ai-powered-protection/azure-bastion?u=76281980&t=59)** Here's a diagram from Microsoft that illustrates the role of Azure Bastion.
>
> **[1:06](https://www.linkedin.com/learning/microsoft-security-essentials-concepts-solutions-and-ai-powered-protection/azure-bastion?u=76281980&t=66)** Instead of directly connecting to a virtual machine through its public IP, you can first log into the Azure portal, then access Azure Bastion in your virtual network.
>
> **[1:19](https://www.linkedin.com/learning/microsoft-security-essentials-concepts-solutions-and-ai-powered-protection/azure-bastion?u=76281980&t=79)** From there, you can connect to your target virtual machine through its private IP.
>
> **[1:26](https://www.linkedin.com/learning/microsoft-security-essentials-concepts-solutions-and-ai-powered-protection/azure-bastion?u=76281980&t=86)** By using Azure Bastion, you can achieve seamless, secure access to your virtual machines without exposing them to public IP addresses.
>
> **[1:36](https://www.linkedin.com/learning/microsoft-security-essentials-concepts-solutions-and-ai-powered-protection/azure-bastion?u=76281980&t=96)** Now, let's do a quick demo of Azure Bastion.

#### Microsoft Defender for Cloud: Workload protection

#### Microsoft Purview Audit
> [LinkedIn Learning](https://www.linkedin.com/learning/microsoft-security-essentials-concepts-solutions-and-ai-powered-protection/microsoft-purview-audit?u=76281980)

> [!transcript]- Transcript
>
> **[0:00](https://www.linkedin.com/learning/microsoft-security-essentials-concepts-solutions-and-ai-powered-protection/microsoft-purview-audit?u=76281980&t=0)** - [Narrator] Audit is a core capability in Microsoft Purview.
>
> **[0:04](https://www.linkedin.com/learning/microsoft-security-essentials-concepts-solutions-and-ai-powered-protection/microsoft-purview-audit?u=76281980&t=4)** It helps organizations gain visibility into activities across their environments.
>
> **[0:10](https://www.linkedin.com/learning/microsoft-security-essentials-concepts-solutions-and-ai-powered-protection/microsoft-purview-audit?u=76281980&t=10)** And it supports data compliance, governance, and security.
>
> **[0:15](https://www.linkedin.com/learning/microsoft-security-essentials-concepts-solutions-and-ai-powered-protection/microsoft-purview-audit?u=76281980&t=15)** The general purpose of an audit is to know who does what, where, and when.
>
> **[0:22](https://www.linkedin.com/learning/microsoft-security-essentials-concepts-solutions-and-ai-powered-protection/microsoft-purview-audit?u=76281980&t=22)** In Microsoft Purview, 'who' usually refers to users and admins.
>
> **[0:27](https://www.linkedin.com/learning/microsoft-security-essentials-concepts-solutions-and-ai-powered-protection/microsoft-purview-audit?u=76281980&t=27)** 'What' refers to activities performed, such as deleted file, updated policy, or reset password.
>
> **[0:36](https://www.linkedin.com/learning/microsoft-security-essentials-concepts-solutions-and-ai-powered-protection/microsoft-purview-audit?u=76281980&t=36)** 'Where' refers to locations or services, such as Microsoft Teams, Exchange, or SharePoint.
>
> **[0:45](https://www.linkedin.com/learning/microsoft-security-essentials-concepts-solutions-and-ai-powered-protection/microsoft-purview-audit?u=76281980&t=45)** 'When' refers to the exact time of an activity happened.
>
> **[0:49](https://www.linkedin.com/learning/microsoft-security-essentials-concepts-solutions-and-ai-powered-protection/microsoft-purview-audit?u=76281980&t=49)** All of this information is captured in a centralized audit log.
>
> **[0:55](https://www.linkedin.com/learning/microsoft-security-essentials-concepts-solutions-and-ai-powered-protection/microsoft-purview-audit?u=76281980&t=55)** Microsoft Purview audit then provides a powerful search tool to help organizations discover the required information.

#### Microsoft Purview Communication Compliance

>
> **[0:10](https://www.linkedin.com/learning/microsoft-security-essentials-concepts-solutions-and-ai-powered-protection/microsoft-purview-communication-compliance?u=76281980&t=10)** Why is communication compliance important?

>
> **[0:57](https://www.linkedin.com/learning/microsoft-security-essentials-concepts-solutions-and-ai-powered-protection/microsoft-purview-communication-compliance?u=76281980&t=57)** Microsoft Purview provides the communication compliance solution to address these concerns.

#### Microsoft Purview Data Lifecycle Management

> **[0:06](https://www.linkedin.com/learning/microsoft-security-essentials-concepts-solutions-and-ai-powered-protection/microsoft-purview-data-lifecycle-management?u=76281980&t=6)** You may wonder, what is data lifecycle management?
>
> **[0:10](https://www.linkedin.com/learning/microsoft-security-essentials-concepts-solutions-and-ai-powered-protection/microsoft-purview-data-lifecycle-management?u=76281980&t=10)** The data lifecycle is the process that data follows, from its creation and storage, to its use, archiving, and eventually deletion.
>
> **[0:21](https://www.linkedin.com/learning/microsoft-security-essentials-concepts-solutions-and-ai-powered-protection/microsoft-purview-data-lifecycle-management?u=76281980&t=21)** Data lifecycle management focuses on two key actions.
>
> **[0:25](https://www.linkedin.com/learning/microsoft-security-essentials-concepts-solutions-and-ai-powered-protection/microsoft-purview-data-lifecycle-management?u=76281980&t=25)** Retain the content that you need.
>
> **[0:28](https://www.linkedin.com/learning/microsoft-security-essentials-concepts-solutions-and-ai-powered-protection/microsoft-purview-data-lifecycle-management?u=76281980&t=28)** For example, keeping some documents for 10 years due to the relevant compliance requirements.
>
> **[0:35](https://www.linkedin.com/learning/microsoft-security-essentials-concepts-solutions-and-ai-powered-protection/microsoft-purview-data-lifecycle-management?u=76281980&t=35)** Delete the content that you don't need.
>
> **[0:37](https://www.linkedin.com/learning/microsoft-security-essentials-concepts-solutions-and-ai-powered-protection/microsoft-purview-data-lifecycle-management?u=76281980&t=37)** For example, deleting archived files after 7 years.
>
> **[0:41](https://www.linkedin.com/learning/microsoft-security-essentials-concepts-solutions-and-ai-powered-protection/microsoft-purview-data-lifecycle-management?u=76281980&t=41)** This helps reduce the amount of data the company manages, and from a security perspective, minimizes the potential attack surface.
>
> **[0:52](https://www.linkedin.com/learning/microsoft-security-essentials-concepts-solutions-and-ai-powered-protection/microsoft-purview-data-lifecycle-management?u=76281980&t=52)** In Microsoft Purview, there are two main methods to manage the data lifecycle.
>
> **[0:57](https://www.linkedin.com/learning/microsoft-security-essentials-concepts-solutions-and-ai-powered-protection/microsoft-purview-data-lifecycle-management?u=76281980&t=57)** Retention policies and retention labels.
>
> **[1:03](https://www.linkedin.com/learning/microsoft-security-essentials-concepts-solutions-and-ai-powered-protection/microsoft-purview-data-lifecycle-management?u=76281980&t=63)** The main difference between them is the scope of coverage.
>
> **[1:07](https://www.linkedin.com/learning/microsoft-security-essentials-concepts-solutions-and-ai-powered-protection/microsoft-purview-data-lifecycle-management?u=76281980&t=67)** A retention policy applies at the site or mailbox level, while a retention label applies to a specific folder, file, or email message.
>
> **[1:18](https://www.linkedin.com/learning/microsoft-security-essentials-concepts-solutions-and-ai-powered-protection/microsoft-purview-data-lifecycle-management?u=76281980&t=78)** You can combine these methods in your data lifecycle management.
>
> **[1:22](https://www.linkedin.com/learning/microsoft-security-essentials-concepts-solutions-and-ai-powered-protection/microsoft-purview-data-lifecycle-management?u=76281980&t=82)** For example, you can create a retention policy for a SharePoint site to retain all content for 7 years, while assigning a retention label to specific files on the SharePoint site to keep them for 10 years.
>
> **[1:37](https://www.linkedin.com/learning/microsoft-security-essentials-concepts-solutions-and-ai-powered-protection/microsoft-purview-data-lifecycle-management?u=76281980&t=97)** You may ask, what happens if I edit or delete a file within the retention period?
>
> **[1:43](https://www.linkedin.com/learning/microsoft-security-essentials-concepts-solutions-and-ai-powered-protection/microsoft-purview-data-lifecycle-management?u=76281980&t=103)** In most cases, you can edit or delete content as usual.
>
> **[1:48](https://www.linkedin.com/learning/microsoft-security-essentials-concepts-solutions-and-ai-powered-protection/microsoft-purview-data-lifecycle-management?u=76281980&t=108)** However, the data lifecycle management will automatically retain a copy of the item in a secure location.
>
> **[1:55](https://www.linkedin.com/learning/microsoft-security-essentials-concepts-solutions-and-ai-powered-protection/microsoft-purview-data-lifecycle-management?u=76281980&t=115)** Now, let's do a quick demo of data lifecycle management.
>
> **[2:01](https://www.linkedin.com/learning/microsoft-security-essentials-concepts-solutions-and-ai-powered-protection/microsoft-purview-data-lifecycle-management?u=76281980&t=121)** Here's the Microsoft Purview portal.
>
> **[2:04](https://www.linkedin.com/learning/microsoft-security-essentials-concepts-solutions-and-ai-powered-protection/microsoft-purview-data-lifecycle-management?u=76281980&t=124)** Let's choose the data lifecycle management solution.
>
> **[2:10](https://www.linkedin.com/learning/microsoft-security-essentials-concepts-solutions-and-ai-powered-protection/microsoft-purview-data-lifecycle-management?u=76281980&t=130)** Under Policies, select retention policies.
>
> **[2:15](https://www.linkedin.com/learning/microsoft-security-essentials-concepts-solutions-and-ai-powered-protection/microsoft-purview-data-lifecycle-management?u=76281980&t=135)** Here you can manage existing policies or create a new one.
>
> **[2:19](https://www.linkedin.com/learning/microsoft-security-essentials-concepts-solutions-and-ai-powered-protection/microsoft-purview-data-lifecycle-management?u=76281980&t=139)** Let's select a policy.
>
> **[2:23](https://www.linkedin.com/learning/microsoft-security-essentials-concepts-solutions-and-ai-powered-protection/microsoft-purview-data-lifecycle-management?u=76281980&t=143)** You can see this policy applies to content in SharePoint sites.
>
> **[2:28](https://www.linkedin.com/learning/microsoft-security-essentials-concepts-solutions-and-ai-powered-protection/microsoft-purview-data-lifecycle-management?u=76281980&t=148)** The retention period is 7 years.
>
> **[2:33](https://www.linkedin.com/learning/microsoft-security-essentials-concepts-solutions-and-ai-powered-protection/microsoft-purview-data-lifecycle-management?u=76281980&t=153)** Now let's look at retention labels.
>
> **[2:37](https://www.linkedin.com/learning/microsoft-security-essentials-concepts-solutions-and-ai-powered-protection/microsoft-purview-data-lifecycle-management?u=76281980&t=157)** Select a label.
>
> **[2:39](https://www.linkedin.com/learning/microsoft-security-essentials-concepts-solutions-and-ai-powered-protection/microsoft-purview-data-lifecycle-management?u=76281980&t=159)** You can see the retention duration is 10 years.

#### Microsoft Purview Records Management

>
> **[0:10](https://www.linkedin.com/learning/microsoft-security-essentials-concepts-solutions-and-ai-powered-protection/microsoft-purview-records-management?u=76281980&t=10)** You may ask, what is a record?

> **[0:17](https://www.linkedin.com/learning/microsoft-security-essentials-concepts-solutions-and-ai-powered-protection/microsoft-purview-records-management?u=76281980&t=17)** When content such as a file, image, or email is labeled as a record, activities on this content are restricted.
>
> **[0:27](https://www.linkedin.com/learning/microsoft-security-essentials-concepts-solutions-and-ai-powered-protection/microsoft-purview-records-management?u=76281980&t=27)** For example, a locked record doesn't allow editing or deletion.

>
> **[0:44](https://www.linkedin.com/learning/microsoft-security-essentials-concepts-solutions-and-ai-powered-protection/microsoft-purview-records-management?u=76281980&t=44)** Records management enables organizations to tighten control over business critical records and meet various regulatory compliance requirements.

### 10. 9. Data Security and Governance

#### Data security and governance with Microsoft Purview
> [LinkedIn Learning](https://www.linkedin.com/learning/microsoft-security-essentials-concepts-solutions-and-ai-powered-protection/data-security-and-governance-with-microsoft-purview?u=76281980)

> **[0:00](https://www.linkedin.com/learning/microsoft-security-essentials-concepts-solutions-and-ai-powered-protection/data-security-and-governance-with-microsoft-purview?u=76281980&t=0)** - [Instructor] Data plays a critical role in the success of businesses today.
>
> **[0:05](https://www.linkedin.com/learning/microsoft-security-essentials-concepts-solutions-and-ai-powered-protection/data-security-and-governance-with-microsoft-purview?u=76281980&t=5)** Let's look at the data security and the data governance capabilities provided by Microsoft Purview.
>
> **[0:12](https://www.linkedin.com/learning/microsoft-security-essentials-concepts-solutions-and-ai-powered-protection/data-security-and-governance-with-microsoft-purview?u=76281980&t=12)** Data security focuses on protecting sensitive information and reducing security risks.
>
> **[0:18](https://www.linkedin.com/learning/microsoft-security-essentials-concepts-solutions-and-ai-powered-protection/data-security-and-governance-with-microsoft-purview?u=76281980&t=18)** Microsoft Purview provides a set of data security solutions such as: information protection to discover, classify, and secure sensitive information across your organization, data loss prevention to detect suspicious behavior and prevent unauthorized disclosure of sensitive information, and insider risk management to identify, investigate, and minimize internal risks.
>
> **[0:49](https://www.linkedin.com/learning/microsoft-security-essentials-concepts-solutions-and-ai-powered-protection/data-security-and-governance-with-microsoft-purview?u=76281980&t=49)** Data governance helps organizations effectively manage, control, and use their enterprise data to enhance data visibility, secure access, and generate business value.
>
> **[1:01](https://www.linkedin.com/learning/microsoft-security-essentials-concepts-solutions-and-ai-powered-protection/data-security-and-governance-with-microsoft-purview?u=76281980&t=61)** Microsoft Purview enables organizations to federate their data governance, distributing data ownership to business units and empowering them to discover the data that they need for the business, have the right data access, ensure data is usable and secure through data curation, which refers to organizing, annotating, and publishing data, ensure data health to have high-quality data, and enhance data understanding by adding helpful descriptors.
>
> **[1:39](https://www.linkedin.com/learning/microsoft-security-essentials-concepts-solutions-and-ai-powered-protection/data-security-and-governance-with-microsoft-purview?u=76281980&t=99)** Microsoft Purview also helps organizations assign clear data roles and responsibilities such as: data owner, who is responsible for specific data assets, data steward, who ensures data quality, consistency, and compliance, data custodian, who manages the technical environment and the data infrastructure, data consumer, who accesses and uses data, and central data office, who sets governance policies and standards.
>
> **[2:14](https://www.linkedin.com/learning/microsoft-security-essentials-concepts-solutions-and-ai-powered-protection/data-security-and-governance-with-microsoft-purview?u=76281980&t=134)** Now let's take a quick tour of Microsoft Purview data security and governance solutions.
>

> **[2:25](https://www.linkedin.com/learning/microsoft-security-essentials-concepts-solutions-and-ai-powered-protection/data-security-and-governance-with-microsoft-purview?u=76281980&t=145)** Let's explore its solutions.
>

>
> **[2:43](https://www.linkedin.com/learning/microsoft-security-essentials-concepts-solutions-and-ai-powered-protection/data-security-and-governance-with-microsoft-purview?u=76281980&t=163)** For data security, it offers solutions like data loss prevention for preventing unauthorized disclosure of sensitive content, information protection for discovering, classifying, and protecting sensitive and business critical information, and insider risk management for detecting risky user activity and then responding to insider threats.

#### Microsoft Purview Information Protection
> [LinkedIn Learning](https://www.linkedin.com/learning/microsoft-security-essentials-concepts-solutions-and-ai-powered-protection/microsoft-purview-information-protection?u=76281980)

> [!transcript]- Transcript
>
> **[0:00](https://www.linkedin.com/learning/microsoft-security-essentials-concepts-solutions-and-ai-powered-protection/microsoft-purview-information-protection?u=76281980&t=0)** - [Instructor] Protecting sensitive and business-critical information is essential for maintaining data security.
>
> **[0:07](https://www.linkedin.com/learning/microsoft-security-essentials-concepts-solutions-and-ai-powered-protection/microsoft-purview-information-protection?u=76281980&t=7)** Let's look at the Information Protection solution provided by Microsoft Purview.
>
> **[0:12](https://www.linkedin.com/learning/microsoft-security-essentials-concepts-solutions-and-ai-powered-protection/microsoft-purview-information-protection?u=76281980&t=12)** To protect your data, you must first understand it in order to identify important information.
>
> **[0:21](https://www.linkedin.com/learning/microsoft-security-essentials-concepts-solutions-and-ai-powered-protection/microsoft-purview-information-protection?u=76281980&t=21)** This process is commonly known as data classification.
>
> **[0:25](https://www.linkedin.com/learning/microsoft-security-essentials-concepts-solutions-and-ai-powered-protection/microsoft-purview-information-protection?u=76281980&t=25)** Microsoft Purview offers several types of classifiers to identify data.
>
> **[0:31](https://www.linkedin.com/learning/microsoft-security-essentials-concepts-solutions-and-ai-powered-protection/microsoft-purview-information-protection?u=76281980&t=31)** Trainable classifiers.
>
> **[0:33](https://www.linkedin.com/learning/microsoft-security-essentials-concepts-solutions-and-ai-powered-protection/microsoft-purview-information-protection?u=76281980&t=33)** These use artificial intelligence to classify your data.
>
> **[0:37](https://www.linkedin.com/learning/microsoft-security-essentials-concepts-solutions-and-ai-powered-protection/microsoft-purview-information-protection?u=76281980&t=37)** Microsoft provides many pre-trained classifiers, such as bank statement, credit report, and invoice.
>
> **[0:46](https://www.linkedin.com/learning/microsoft-security-essentials-concepts-solutions-and-ai-powered-protection/microsoft-purview-information-protection?u=76281980&t=46)** You can also create a custom trainable classifiers for your specific business data.
>
> **[0:51](https://www.linkedin.com/learning/microsoft-security-essentials-concepts-solutions-and-ai-powered-protection/microsoft-purview-information-protection?u=76281980&t=51)** Trainable classifiers are used to classify items like files or email messages.
>
> **[0:58](https://www.linkedin.com/learning/microsoft-security-essentials-concepts-solutions-and-ai-powered-protection/microsoft-purview-information-protection?u=76281980&t=58)** To further identify the elements within those items, you can use sensitive information types.
>
> **[1:06](https://www.linkedin.com/learning/microsoft-security-essentials-concepts-solutions-and-ai-powered-protection/microsoft-purview-information-protection?u=76281980&t=66)** These are pattern-based classifiers.
>
> **[1:09](https://www.linkedin.com/learning/microsoft-security-essentials-concepts-solutions-and-ai-powered-protection/microsoft-purview-information-protection?u=76281980&t=69)** For example, they can detect credit card numbers, social security numbers, or bank account numbers based on specific patterns.
>
> **[1:19](https://www.linkedin.com/learning/microsoft-security-essentials-concepts-solutions-and-ai-powered-protection/microsoft-purview-information-protection?u=76281980&t=79)** You can also use exact values from your organization's data to detect matches instead of relying on generic patterns.
>
> **[1:28](https://www.linkedin.com/learning/microsoft-security-essentials-concepts-solutions-and-ai-powered-protection/microsoft-purview-information-protection?u=76281980&t=88)** These are known as exact data match, or EDM classifiers.
>
> **[1:35](https://www.linkedin.com/learning/microsoft-security-essentials-concepts-solutions-and-ai-powered-protection/microsoft-purview-information-protection?u=76281980&t=95)** Microsoft Purview also enables you to label sensitive data.
>
> **[1:40](https://www.linkedin.com/learning/microsoft-security-essentials-concepts-solutions-and-ai-powered-protection/microsoft-purview-information-protection?u=76281980&t=100)** First, you need to create a variance of sensitivity labels based on the sensitivity levels defined by your organization, such as personal, public, confidential, and highly confidential.
>
> **[1:53](https://www.linkedin.com/learning/microsoft-security-essentials-concepts-solutions-and-ai-powered-protection/microsoft-purview-information-protection?u=76281980&t=113)** Once created, this sensitivity labels are published through label policies, which define rules such as which users and groups that can see labels, the default label to be applied, whether justifications are required for label changes, and whether a sensitivity label must be applied before saving documents.
>
> **[2:17](https://www.linkedin.com/learning/microsoft-security-essentials-concepts-solutions-and-ai-powered-protection/microsoft-purview-information-protection?u=76281980&t=137)** To bring visibility to sensitive content across your organization's environment, Microsoft Purview provides data and content explorer to discover documents and emails that contains sensitive information or have a sensitivity labels applied, and activity explorer to review activities related to sensitive content.
>
> **[2:42](https://www.linkedin.com/learning/microsoft-security-essentials-concepts-solutions-and-ai-powered-protection/microsoft-purview-information-protection?u=76281980&t=162)** Now let's do a quick demo of Microsoft Purview Information Protection.
>
> **[2:49](https://www.linkedin.com/learning/microsoft-security-essentials-concepts-solutions-and-ai-powered-protection/microsoft-purview-information-protection?u=76281980&t=169)** Here's the Microsoft Purview portal.
>
> **[2:52](https://www.linkedin.com/learning/microsoft-security-essentials-concepts-solutions-and-ai-powered-protection/microsoft-purview-information-protection?u=76281980&t=172)** Let's choose the Information Protection solution.
>
> **[3:00](https://www.linkedin.com/learning/microsoft-security-essentials-concepts-solutions-and-ai-powered-protection/microsoft-purview-information-protection?u=76281980&t=180)** Under Classifiers, you can see Trainable classifiers.
>
> **[3:04](https://www.linkedin.com/learning/microsoft-security-essentials-concepts-solutions-and-ai-powered-protection/microsoft-purview-information-protection?u=76281980&t=184)** These are building or custom classifiers to identify common items such as bank statements, budget, or business plan.
>
> **[3:14](https://www.linkedin.com/learning/microsoft-security-essentials-concepts-solutions-and-ai-powered-protection/microsoft-purview-information-protection?u=76281980&t=194)** Sensitive info types.
>
> **[3:17](https://www.linkedin.com/learning/microsoft-security-essentials-concepts-solutions-and-ai-powered-protection/microsoft-purview-information-protection?u=76281980&t=197)** This match content elements based on patterns, such as full name, physical address, and passport number.
>
> **[3:30](https://www.linkedin.com/learning/microsoft-security-essentials-concepts-solutions-and-ai-powered-protection/microsoft-purview-information-protection?u=76281980&t=210)** EDM classifiers.
>
> **[3:32](https://www.linkedin.com/learning/microsoft-security-essentials-concepts-solutions-and-ai-powered-protection/microsoft-purview-information-protection?u=76281980&t=212)** These use exact values to detect matches rather than patterns.
>

### 11. 10. Privacy Protection

#### Privacy protection with Microsoft Priva

> **[0:00](https://www.linkedin.com/learning/microsoft-security-essentials-concepts-solutions-and-ai-powered-protection/privacy-protection-with-microsoft-priva?u=76281980&t=0)** - [Instructor] Privacy has become a major concern in today's business world.
>
> **[0:05](https://www.linkedin.com/learning/microsoft-security-essentials-concepts-solutions-and-ai-powered-protection/privacy-protection-with-microsoft-priva?u=76281980&t=5)** It goes beyond meeting regulatory requirements.

> **[0:07](https://www.linkedin.com/learning/microsoft-security-essentials-concepts-solutions-and-ai-powered-protection/privacy-protection-with-microsoft-priva?u=76281980&t=7)** It's essential for building organizational trust.

> **[0:12](https://www.linkedin.com/learning/microsoft-security-essentials-concepts-solutions-and-ai-powered-protection/privacy-protection-with-microsoft-priva?u=76281980&t=12)** Now let's look at the privacy protection capabilities provided by Microsoft Priva.
>
> **[0:18](https://www.linkedin.com/learning/microsoft-security-essentials-concepts-solutions-and-ai-powered-protection/privacy-protection-with-microsoft-priva?u=76281980&t=18)** The core of a privacy protection is processing personal data lawfully, fairly and transparently.
>
> **[0:25](https://www.linkedin.com/learning/microsoft-security-essentials-concepts-solutions-and-ai-powered-protection/privacy-protection-with-microsoft-priva?u=76281980&t=25)** It covers consent and collection.
>
> **[0:28](https://www.linkedin.com/learning/microsoft-security-essentials-concepts-solutions-and-ai-powered-protection/privacy-protection-with-microsoft-priva?u=76281980&t=28)** Before collecting personal data, you must obtain clear consent from individuals so they understand what data you are collecting and for what purposes.
>
> **[0:38](https://www.linkedin.com/learning/microsoft-security-essentials-concepts-solutions-and-ai-powered-protection/privacy-protection-with-microsoft-priva?u=76281980&t=38)** Also, only collect data that is necessary to minimize risks.
>
> **[0:43](https://www.linkedin.com/learning/microsoft-security-essentials-concepts-solutions-and-ai-powered-protection/privacy-protection-with-microsoft-priva?u=76281980&t=43)** Storage and transfer.
>
> **[0:45](https://www.linkedin.com/learning/microsoft-security-essentials-concepts-solutions-and-ai-powered-protection/privacy-protection-with-microsoft-priva?u=76281980&t=45)** You must store personal data securely using technologies like encryption.
>
> **[0:50](https://www.linkedin.com/learning/microsoft-security-essentials-concepts-solutions-and-ai-powered-protection/privacy-protection-with-microsoft-priva?u=76281980&t=50)** When transferring data, you must prevent data leaks and complying with applicable legal and regulatory requirements, such as cross-border data transfer rules.
>
> **[1:02](https://www.linkedin.com/learning/microsoft-security-essentials-concepts-solutions-and-ai-powered-protection/privacy-protection-with-microsoft-priva?u=76281980&t=62)** Data access.
>
> **[1:03](https://www.linkedin.com/learning/microsoft-security-essentials-concepts-solutions-and-ai-powered-protection/privacy-protection-with-microsoft-priva?u=76281980&t=63)** You must limit access to sensitive personal information and prevent unauthorized disclosure.
>
> **[1:10](https://www.linkedin.com/learning/microsoft-security-essentials-concepts-solutions-and-ai-powered-protection/privacy-protection-with-microsoft-priva?u=76281980&t=70)** Data sharing.
>

#### Microsoft Priva Subject Rights Requests
> [LinkedIn Learning](https://www.linkedin.com/learning/microsoft-security-essentials-concepts-solutions-and-ai-powered-protection/microsoft-priva-subject-rights-requests?u=76281980)

> [!transcript]- Transcript
